***трамвай.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́й</a> (3363)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tramway</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tramway</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg/220px-Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="138" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg/330px-Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/65/Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg/440px-Nagatino-Sadovniki_tram_on_NagatinskayaStreet_img2_05-2015.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5360" data-file-height="3350" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́й</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tramváj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трамвай.html>трамва́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tram, tramway <i>(GB)</i></li>
<li>streetcar, trolley, trolley car, light rail <i>(USA)</i></li></ol>

***трамплин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трамплин.html>трампли́н</a> (27627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tremplin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">trempellino</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">trempellare</i>, from an unidentified <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> form. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">trampeln</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">trample</i>.
</p><p>Attested since 1830.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транс.html>транс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trans</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транс.html>тра́нса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транс.html>тра́нсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транс.html>тра́нсов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:транслировать.html>трансли́ровать</a> (26143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Evidently backformed from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">transljácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">trānslatiō</i>), with the suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транслировать.html>трансли́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">translírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to transmit, to broadcast, to relay</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to translate, to compile</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транслятор.html>трансля́тор</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">transljátor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">transljácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">трансляцио́нный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">transljaciónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ретрансли́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">retranslírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***трансляция.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ция</a> (17019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">trānslātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">transljácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трансляция.html>трансля́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>broadcast, transmission, translation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a radio or TV transmission on air</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">transporter</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транспорт.html>тра́нспорт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tránsport</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транспортный.html>тра́нспортный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tránsportnyj</span>)
</p>

***трата.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́та</a> (15381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tráta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>expenditure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:денежный.html>де́нежная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dénežnaja <b>tráta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">expense</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустой.html>пуста́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трата.html>тра́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pustája <b>tráta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">waste (of something)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тратить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тратить.html>тра́тить</a> (3190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тратить.html>тра́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trátitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истратить.html>истра́тить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потратить.html>потра́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend, to expend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тратить.html>тра́тить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trátitʹ</b> dénʹgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spend money</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to waste</li>
<li>to fritter away (time)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тратить.html>тра́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trátitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тратиться.html>тра́титься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trátitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">истра́титься</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">потра́титься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend money, to spend up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тратить.html>тра́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trátitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
